NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

CORVESTA SOFTWARE SOLUTIONS INDIA PRIVATE LIMITED
Regd. Off: Suite 305, Delta Wing, 3rd Floor, Raheja Towers,
No.177, Anna Salai, Chennai-600 002, Tamil Nadu
In the matter of Section 485 of Companies Act, 1956 and Rule 315 of
The Companies (Court) Rules, 1959
Notice of Appointment of Liquidator

Notice is hereby given to the General Public that the shareholders of the Company at the extra ordinary general meeting
held on 1st Day of July, 2016 at 11 AM has passed the following resolution for voluntary winding up of the Company under
Section 484 and 490 under the Companies Act, 1956 and has also appointed M/s. Krishnaji Rao Chandra Pratap, as the
liquidator of the company, who has forthwith taken over the affairs of the company and initiate proceeding to wind up the
company.
Resolution passed by the Shareholders:
“RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provisions of Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, consent of the members
of the Company be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the Company as members’ voluntary winding up, with
effect from 1st July 2016.”
